* Psalms 1

** Psalms 1:1

Beatus vir qui non abiit in consilio impiorum, <l eID="gen4557" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4558"/>et in via peccatorum non stetit, <l eID="gen4558" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4559"/>et in cathedra pestilentiæ non sedit ; <l eID="gen4559" level="1"/>

** Psalms 1:2

sed in lege Domini voluntas ejus, <l eID="gen4560" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4561"/>et in lege ejus meditabitur die ac nocte. <l eID="gen4561" level="1"/>

** Psalms 1:3

Et erit tamquam lignum quod plantatum est secus decursus aquarum, <l eID="gen4562" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4563"/>quod fructum suum dabit in tempore suo : <l eID="gen4563" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4564"/>et folium ejus non defluet ; <l eID="gen4564" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4565"/>et omnia quæcumque faciet prosperabuntur. <l eID="gen4565" level="1"/>

** Psalms 1:4

Non sic impii, non sic ; <l eID="gen4566" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4567"/>sed tamquam pulvis quem projicit ventus a facie terræ. <l eID="gen4567" level="1"/>

** Psalms 1:5

Ideo non resurgent impii in judicio, <l eID="gen4568" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4569"/>neque peccatores in concilio justorum : <l eID="gen4569" level="1"/>

** Psalms 1:6

quoniam novit Dominus viam justorum, <l eID="gen4570" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen4571"/>et iter impiorum peribit.  <chapter eID="Ps.1"/>

** Psalms 2:13

** Psalms 4:5

** Psalms 4:6

** Psalms 4:7

** Psalms 4:8

** Psalms 4:9

** Psalms 5:12

* Psalms 78

** Psalms 78:1

Psalmus Asaph. <div eID="gen7535" type="x-p"/> <lg sID="gen7536"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7537"/>Deus, venerunt gentes in hæreditatem tuam ; <l eID="gen7537" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7538"/>polluerunt templum sanctum tuum ; <l eID="gen7538" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7539"/>posuerunt Jerusalem in pomorum custodiam. <l eID="gen7539" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:2

Posuerunt morticina servorum tuorum escas volatilibus cæli ; <l eID="gen7540" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7541"/>carnes sanctorum tuorum bestiis terræ. <l eID="gen7541" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:3

Effuderunt sanguinem eorum tamquam aquam in circuitu Jerusalem, <l eID="gen7542" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7543"/>et non erat qui sepeliret. <l eID="gen7543" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:4

Facti sumus opprobrium vicinis nostris ; <l eID="gen7544" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7545"/>subsannatio et illusio his qui in circuitu nostro sunt. <l eID="gen7545" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:5

Usquequo, Domine, irasceris in finem ? <l eID="gen7546" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7547"/>accendetur velut ignis zelus tuus ? <l eID="gen7547" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:6

Effunde iram tuam in gentes quæ te non noverunt, <l eID="gen7548" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7549"/>et in regna quæ nomen tuum non invocaverunt : <l eID="gen7549" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:7

quia comederunt Jacob, <l eID="gen7550" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7551"/>et locum ejus desolaverunt. <l eID="gen7551" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:8

Ne memineris iniquitatum nostrarum antiquarum ; <l eID="gen7552" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7553"/>cito anticipent nos misericordiæ tuæ, <l eID="gen7553" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7554"/>quia pauperes facti sumus nimis. <l eID="gen7554" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:9

Adjuva nos, Deus salutaris noster, <l eID="gen7555" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7556"/>et propter gloriam nominis tui, Domine, libera nos : <l eID="gen7556" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7557"/>et propitius esto peccatis nostris, propter nomen tuum. <l eID="gen7557" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:10

Ne forte dicant in gentibus : Ubi est Deus eorum ? <l eID="gen7558" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7559"/>et innotescat in nationibus coram oculis nostris <l eID="gen7559" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7560"/>ultio sanguinis servorum tuorum qui effusus est. <l eID="gen7560" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:11

Introëat in conspectu tuo gemitus compeditorum ; <l eID="gen7561" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7562"/>secundum magnitudinem brachii tui posside filios mortificatorum : <l eID="gen7562" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:12

et redde vicinis nostris septuplum in sinu eorum ; <l eID="gen7563" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7564"/>improperium ipsorum quod exprobraverunt tibi, Domine. <l eID="gen7564" level="1"/>

** Psalms 78:13

* Psalms 79

** Psalms 79:1

** Psalms 79:9

Vineam de Ægypto transtulisti : <l eID="gen7586" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7587"/>ejecisti gentes, et plantasti eam. <l eID="gen7587" level="1"/>

** Psalms 79:10

Dux itineris fuisti in conspectu ejus ; <l eID="gen7588" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7589"/>plantasti radices ejus, et implevit terram. <l eID="gen7589" level="1"/>

** Psalms 79:13

** Psalms 79:14

Exterminavit eam aper de silva, <l eID="gen7596" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7597"/>et singularis ferus depastus est eam. <l eID="gen7597" level="1"/>

** Psalms 79:15

Deus virtutum, convertere, <l eID="gen7598" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7599"/>respice de cælo, et vide, <l eID="gen7599" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7600"/>et visita vineam istam : <l eID="gen7600" level="1"/>

** Psalms 79:16

et perfice eam quam plantavit dextera tua, <l eID="gen7601" level="1"/> <l level="1" sID="gen7602"/>et super filium hominis quem confirmasti tibi. <l eID="gen7602" level="1"/>

** Psalms 79:17

** Psalms 79:18

** Psalms 79:19

** Psalms 80:13

** Psalms 80:14

** Psalms 80:15

* Psalms 119

** Psalms 119:1
